  for (const auto& [factory_name, factory] : factories()) {\n      UNREFERENCED_PARAMETER(factory_name);\n      if (factory == nullptr) {\n        continue;\n      }\n\n      for (const auto& config_type : factory->configTypes()) {\n        ASSERT(!config_type.empty(), \"Extension config types can never be empty string\");\n\n        // Register config types in the mapping.\n        auto https://github.com/envoyproxy/envoy/issues/9643.\n          RELEASE_ASSERT(false, fmt::format(\"Double registration for type: '{}' by '{}' and '{}'\",\n                                            config_type, factory->name(),\n                                            it->second ? it->second->name() : \"\"));\n          it->second = nullptr;\n        } else {\n          mapping->emplace(std::make_pair(config_type, factory));\n        }\n      }\n    }\n\n    return mapping;\n  }\n\n  // Rebuild the factories-by-type map based on the current factories.\n  static void rebuildFactoriesByTypeForTest() {\n    auto& mapping = factoriesByType();\n    auto updated_mapping = buildFactoriesByType();\n\n    // Copy the updated mapping over the old one.\n    mapping = *updated_mapping;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Replaces a factory by name.                        std::initializer_list<absl::string_view> deprecated_names = {}) {\n    using DeprecatedNamesVector = std::vector<std::pair<std::string, std::string>>;\n\n    // If an existing factory is registered with this name, track it for later restoration.\n    Base* prev_by_name = nullptr;\n    auto it = factories().find(factory.name());\n    if (it != factories().end()) {\n      prev_by_name = it->second;\n      factories().erase(it);\n\n      ENVOY_LOG(\n          info, \"Factory '{}' (type '{}') displaced-by-name with test factory '{}' (type '{}')\",\n          prev_by_name->name(), prev_by_name->configTypes(), factory.name(), factory.configTypes());\n    } else {\n      ENVOY_LOG(info, \"Factory '{}' (type '{}') registered for tests\", factory.name(),\n                factory.configTypes());\n    }\n\n    factories().emplace(factory.name(), &factory);\n    RELEASE_ASSERT(getFactory(factory.name()) == &factory,\n                   \"test factory by-name deprecatedFactoryNames().erase(it);\n\n          ENVOY_LOG(\n              info,\n              \"Deprecated name '{}' (mapped to '{}') displaced with test factory '{}' (type '{}')\",\n              it->first, it->second, factory.name(), factory.configTypes());\n        } else {\n          // Name not previously mapped, remember to remove it.\n          prev_deprecated_names.emplace_back(std::make_pair(deprecated_name, \"\"));\n\n          ENVOY_LOG(info, \"Deprecated name '{}' (mapped to '{}')\", deprecated_name, factory.name());\n        }\n\n        // Register the replacement factory with a deprecated name.\n        factories().emplace(deprecated_name, &factory);\n        RELEASE_ASSERT(getFactory(deprecated_name) == &factory,\n                       \"test factory registration by deprecated name failed\");\n\n        // Register the replacement factory's deprecated name.\n        deprecatedFactoryNames().emplace(std::make_pair(deprecated_name, factory.name()));\n      }\n    }\n\n    rebuildFactoriesByTypeForTest();\n\n    return [replacement = &factory, prev_by_name, prev_deprecated_names]() {\n      // Unregister the replacement factory by name.\n      factories().erase(replacement->name());\n\n      ENVOY_LOG(info, \"Removed test factory '{}' (type '{}')\", Overview\\nEnvoy's HTTP filter system uses a factory pattern with compile-time and runtime registration mechanisms. Filters are registered via factories, built into filter chains at configuration time, and instantiated per-request at runtime.\\n\\n## 1. Filter Factory Registry\\nThe core registry is implemented in `envoy/registry/registry.h`:\\n- **FactoryRegistry<Base>**: A template class that maintains a static map of factories by name\\n  - `getFactory(name)`: Retrieves a registered factory by name\\n  - `registerFactory()`: Registers a factory instance\\n  - `factories()`: Returns the static factory map\\n\\n- **RegisterFactory<T, Base>**: A template class used for static registration\\n  - Constructor automatically registers the factory instance when instantiated\\n  - Typically instantiated via `REGISTER_FACTORY(ConcreteFactory, BaseFactory)` macros\\n  - Also registers the factory's category via `FactoryCategoryRegistry`\\n\\n## 2. HTTP Filter Factory Interface\\nDefined in `envoy/server/filter_config.h`:\\n- **NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory**: The base interface for HTTP filter factories\\n  - Extends `HttpFilterConfigFactoryBase` and `ProtocolOptionsFactory`\\n  - `createFilterFactoryFromProto()`: Creates a `FilterFactoryCb` (per-connection filter factory function) from protobuf config\\n  - Returns `absl::StatusOr<Http::FilterFactoryCb>` to allow error handling\\n  - Each filter implementation inherits from this and implements the factory method\\n\\n## 3. Filter Chain Creation (Configuration Time)\\nAt server startup, the configuration system builds the HTTP filter chain:\\n\\n**FilterChainHelper** (`source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.h`):\\n- `FilterChainHelper::processFilters()`: Iterates over protobuf filter configurations\\n  - For each filter config, looks up the factory via `Config::Utility::getAndCheckFactory<NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory>`\\n  - Calls `factory->createFilterFactoryFromProto()` to get the `FilterFactoryCb`\\n  - Stores the callback in a `FilterConfigProvider`\\n  - Returns a list of `FilterFactoryProvider` objects containing these callbacks\\n\\n**HttpConnectionManagerConfig** (`source/extensions/filters/network/http_connection_manager/config.h`):\\n- Implements `Http::FilterChainFactory` interface\\n- Stores a `FilterFactoriesList` of pre-built filter factories\\n- `createFilterChain()`: Called per-stream to instantiate filters\\n\\n**FilterChainUtility** (`source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.h`):\\n- `createFilterChainForFactories()`: Iterates through the pre-built filter factory list\\n  - For each filter factory, retrieves the cached `FilterFactoryCb`\\n  - Calls `manager.applyFilterFactoryCb()` to apply it per-stream\\n\\n## 4. Per-Request Filter Instantiation (Runtime)\\n\\n**FilterManager** (`source/common/http/filter_manager.h`):\\n- Implements `Http::FilterChainManager` interface\\n- `createFilterChain()`: Called per-HTTP-stream when the first request headers arrive\\n  - Checks if upgrade is requested, delegates to appropriate factory\\n  - Calls `filter_chain_factory_.createFilterChain(*this, ...)`\\n\\n**FilterManager::applyFilterFactoryCb()** (`source/common/http/filter_manager.cc`):\\n- Called for each filter factory callback\\n- Creates a `FilterChainFactoryCallbacksImpl` instance\\n- Invokes the `FilterFactoryCb` function, passing the callbacks object\\n- The callback function creates actual filter instances and registers them via `callbacks.addStreamDecoderFilter()` or `callbacks.addStreamEncoderFilter()`\\n\\n## 5. Filter Factory Implementation Pattern\\n\\n**Factory Base Classes** (`source/extensions/filters/http/common/factory_base.h`):\\n- `FactoryBase<ConfigProto>`: Implements `NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory`\\n  - Handles protobuf downcasting and validation\\n  - Delegates to `createFilterFactoryFromProtoTyped()` for the actual factory function\\n\\n- `DualFactoryBase<ConfigProto>`: Supports both downstream and upstream filter configurations\\n\\n- `ExceptionFreeFactoryBase<ConfigProto>`: Returns `absl::StatusOr` instead of throwing exceptions\\n\\n**Example: BufferFilter** (`source/extensions/filters/http/buffer/config.h`):\\n- `BufferFilterFactory`: Extends `DualFactoryBase`\\n- `createFilterFactoryFromProtoTyped()`: Returns a lambda that creates `BufferFilter` instances\\n  ```cpp\\n  return [filter_config](Http::FilterChainFactoryCallbacks& callbacks) -> void {\\n    callbacks.addStreamDecoderFilter(std::make_shared<BufferFilter>(filter_config));\\n  };\\n  ```\\n- Registration via `REGISTER_FACTORY(BufferFilterFactory, NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory)`\\n\\n## 6. Request Router Filter\\n\\n**Router::FilterConfig** (`source/common/router/router.h`):\\n- Implements `Http::FilterChainFactory` for upstream HTTP filters\\n- `createFilterChain()`: Uses `FilterChainUtility::createFilterChainForFactories()` to build upstream filter chains\\n- Allows filters to be chained between the router and upstream connections\\n\\n## Registration Flow Summary\\n\\n1. **Compile Time**: Filter implementations define factory classes inheriting from `NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory`\\n2. **Static Initialization**: `REGISTER_FACTORY` macro instantiates `RegisterFactory`, which calls `FactoryRegistry<NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory>::registerFactory()`\\n3. **Configuration Time**: Server parses config, `FilterChainHelper` looks up factories by name and calls `createFilterFactoryFromProto()` to create filter callbacks\\n4. **Per-Stream Time**: `FilterManager::createFilterChain()` is called, which invokes cached `FilterFactoryCb` callbacks\\n5. **Per-Stream**: Each callback creates actual filter instances and registers them with `FilterChainManager`\\n\\nThis design separates concerns: factories handle expensive operations (parsing, validation) at configuration time, while actual filter instantiation happens lazily per-stream.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":9,"cache_creation_input_tokens":3472,"cache_read_input_tokens":68359,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":3472},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"f51894fb-3b87-4982-bb16-537c9f5cce15","uuid":"7751b282-71c5-4e0d-b825-e1ee2f0dc1e7"}

\"path\": \"source/common/http/filter_manager.cc\", \"symbol\": \"FilterManager::applyFilterFactoryCb\"}\n  ],\n  \"text\": \"# HTTP Filter Factory Registration and Instantiation in Envoy\\n\\n## Overview\\nEnvoy's HTTP filter system uses a factory pattern with compile-time and runtime registration mechanisms. Filters are registered via factories, built into filter chains at configuration time, and instantiated per-request at runtime.\\n\\n## 1. Filter Factory Registry\\nThe core registry is implemented in `envoy/registry/registry.h`:\\n- **FactoryRegistry<Base>**: A template class that maintains a static map of factories by name\\n  - `getFactory(name)`: Retrieves a registered factory by name\\n  - `registerFactory()`: Registers a factory instance\\n  - `factories()`: Returns the static factory map\\n\\n- **RegisterFactory<T, Base>**: A template class used for static registration\\n  - Constructor automatically registers the factory instance when instantiated\\n  - Typically instantiated via `REGISTER_FACTORY(ConcreteFactory, BaseFactory)` macros\\n  - Also registers the factory's category via `FactoryCategoryRegistry`\\n\\n## 2. HTTP Filter Factory Interface\\nDefined in `envoy/server/filter_config.h`:\\n- **NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory**: The base interface for HTTP filter factories\\n  - Extends `HttpFilterConfigFactoryBase` and `ProtocolOptionsFactory`\\n  - `createFilterFactoryFromProto()`: Creates a `FilterFactoryCb` (per-connection filter factory function) from protobuf config\\n  - Returns `absl::StatusOr<Http::FilterFactoryCb>` to allow error handling\\n  - Each filter implementation inherits from this and implements the factory method\\n\\n## 3. Filter Chain Creation (Configuration Time)\\nAt server startup, the configuration system builds the HTTP filter chain:\\n\\n**FilterChainHelper** (`source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.h`):\\n- `FilterChainHelper::processFilters()`: Iterates over protobuf filter configurations\\n  - For each filter config, looks up the factory via `Config::Utility::getAndCheckFactory<NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory>`\\n  - Calls `factory->createFilterFactoryFromProto()` to get the `FilterFactoryCb`\\n  - Stores the callback in a `FilterConfigProvider`\\n  - Returns a list of `FilterFactoryProvider` objects containing these callbacks\\n\\n**HttpConnectionManagerConfig** (`source/extensions/filters/network/http_connection_manager/config.h`):\\n- Implements `Http::FilterChainFactory` interface\\n- Stores a `FilterFactoriesList` of pre-built filter factories\\n- `createFilterChain()`: Called per-stream to instantiate filters\\n\\n**FilterChainUtility** (`source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.h`):\\n- `createFilterChainForFactories()`: Iterates through the pre-built filter factory list\\n  - For each filter factory, retrieves the cached `FilterFactoryCb`\\n  - Calls `manager.applyFilterFactoryCb()` to apply it per-stream\\n\\n## 4. Per-Request Filter Instantiation (Runtime)\\n\\n**FilterManager** (`source/common/http/filter_manager.h`):\\n- Implements `Http::FilterChainManager` interface\\n- `createFilterChain()`: Called per-HTTP-stream when the first request headers arrive\\n  - Checks if upgrade is requested, delegates to appropriate factory\\n  - Calls `filter_chain_factory_.createFilterChain(*this, ...)`\\n\\n**FilterManager::applyFilterFactoryCb()** (`source/common/http/filter_manager.cc`):\\n- Called for each filter factory callback\\n- Creates a `FilterChainFactoryCallbacksImpl` instance\\n- Invokes the `FilterFactoryCb` function, passing the callbacks object\\n- The callback function creates actual filter instances and registers them via `callbacks.addStreamDecoderFilter()` or `callbacks.addStreamEncoderFilter()`\\n\\n## 5. Filter Factory Implementation Pattern\\n\\n**Factory Base Classes** (`source/extensions/filters/http/common/factory_base.h`):\\n- `FactoryBase<ConfigProto>`: Implements `NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory`\\n  - Handles protobuf downcasting and validation\\n  - Delegates to `createFilterFactoryFromProtoTyped()` for the actual factory function\\n\\n- `DualFactoryBase<ConfigProto>`: Supports both downstream and upstream filter configurations\\n\\n- `ExceptionFreeFactoryBase<ConfigProto>`: Returns `absl::StatusOr` instead of throwing exceptions\\n\\n**Example: BufferFilter** (`source/extensions/filters/http/buffer/config.h`):\\n- `BufferFilterFactory`: Extends `DualFactoryBase`\\n- `createFilterFactoryFromProtoTyped()`: Returns a lambda that creates `BufferFilter` instances\\n  ```cpp\\n  return [filter_config](Http::FilterChainFactoryCallbacks& callbacks) -> void {\\n    callbacks.addStreamDecoderFilter(std::make_shared<BufferFilter>(filter_config));\\n  };\\n  ```\\n- Registration via `REGISTER_FACTORY(BufferFilterFactory, NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory)`\\n\\n## 6. Request Router Filter\\n\\n**Router::FilterConfig** (`source/common/router/router.h`):\\n- Implements `Http::FilterChainFactory` for upstream HTTP filters\\n- `createFilterChain()`: Uses `FilterChainUtility::createFilterChainForFactories()` to build upstream filter chains\\n- Allows filters to be chained between the router and upstream connections\\n\\n## Registration Flow Summary\\n\\n1. **Compile Time**: Filter implementations define factory classes inheriting from `NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory`\\n2. **Static Initialization**: `REGISTER_FACTORY` macro instantiates `RegisterFactory`, which calls `FactoryRegistry<NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory>::registerFactory()`\\n3. **Configuration Time**: Server parses config, `FilterChainHelper` looks up factories by name and calls `createFilterFactoryFromProto()` to create filter callbacks\\n4. **Per-Stream Time**: `FilterManager::createFilterChain()` is called, which invokes cached `FilterFactoryCb` callbacks\\n5. **Per-Stream**: Each callback creates actual filter instances and registers them with `FilterChainManager`\\n\\nThis design separates concerns: factories handle expensive operations (parsing, validation) at configuration time, while actual filter instantiation happens lazily per-stream.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}

Overview\\nEnvoy's HTTP filter system uses a factory pattern with compile-time and runtime registration mechanisms. Filters are registered via factories, built into filter chains at configuration time, and instantiated per-request at runtime.\\n\\n## 1. Filter Factory Registry\\nThe core registry is implemented in `envoy/registry/registry.h`:\\n- **FactoryRegistry<Base>**: A template class that maintains a static map of factories by name\\n  - `getFactory(name)`: Retrieves a registered factory by name\\n  - `registerFactory()`: Registers a factory instance\\n  - `factories()`: Returns the static factory map\\n\\n- **RegisterFactory<T, Base>**: A template class used for static registration\\n  - Constructor automatically registers the factory instance when instantiated\\n  - Typically instantiated via `REGISTER_FACTORY(ConcreteFactory, BaseFactory)` macros\\n  - Also registers the factory's category via `FactoryCategoryRegistry`\\n\\n## 2. HTTP Filter Factory Interface\\nDefined in `envoy/server/filter_config.h`:\\n- **NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory**: The base interface for HTTP filter factories\\n  - Extends `HttpFilterConfigFactoryBase` and `ProtocolOptionsFactory`\\n  - `createFilterFactoryFromProto()`: Creates a `FilterFactoryCb` (per-connection filter factory function) from protobuf config\\n  - Returns `absl::StatusOr<Http::FilterFactoryCb>` to allow error handling\\n  - Each filter implementation inherits from this and implements the factory method\\n\\n## 3. Filter Chain Creation (Configuration Time)\\nAt server startup, the configuration system builds the HTTP filter chain:\\n\\n**FilterChainHelper** (`source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.h`):\\n- `FilterChainHelper::processFilters()`: Iterates over protobuf filter configurations\\n  - For each filter config, looks up the factory via `Config::Utility::getAndCheckFactory<NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory>`\\n  - Calls `factory->createFilterFactoryFromProto()` to get the `FilterFactoryCb`\\n  - Stores the callback in a `FilterConfigProvider`\\n  - Returns a list of `FilterFactoryProvider` objects containing these callbacks\\n\\n**HttpConnectionManagerConfig** (`source/extensions/filters/network/http_connection_manager/config.h`):\\n- Implements `Http::FilterChainFactory` interface\\n- Stores a `FilterFactoriesList` of pre-built filter factories\\n- `createFilterChain()`: Called per-stream to instantiate filters\\n\\n**FilterChainUtility** (`source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.h`):\\n- `createFilterChainForFactories()`: Iterates through the pre-built filter factory list\\n  - For each filter factory, retrieves the cached `FilterFactoryCb`\\n  - Calls `manager.applyFilterFactoryCb()` to apply it per-stream\\n\\n## 4. Per-Request Filter Instantiation (Runtime)\\n\\n**FilterManager** (`source/common/http/filter_manager.h`):\\n- Implements `Http::FilterChainManager` interface\\n- `createFilterChain()`: Called per-HTTP-stream when the first request headers arrive\\n  - Checks if upgrade is requested, delegates to appropriate factory\\n  - Calls `filter_chain_factory_.createFilterChain(*this, ...)`\\n\\n**FilterManager::applyFilterFactoryCb()** (`source/common/http/filter_manager.cc`):\\n- Called for each filter factory callback\\n- Creates a `FilterChainFactoryCallbacksImpl` instance\\n- Invokes the `FilterFactoryCb` function, passing the callbacks object\\n- The callback function creates actual filter instances and registers them via `callbacks.addStreamDecoderFilter()` or `callbacks.addStreamEncoderFilter()`\\n\\n## 5. Filter Factory Implementation Pattern\\n\\n**Factory Base Classes** (`source/extensions/filters/http/common/factory_base.h`):\\n- `FactoryBase<ConfigProto>`: Implements `NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory`\\n  - Handles protobuf downcasting and validation\\n  - Delegates to `createFilterFactoryFromProtoTyped()` for the actual factory function\\n\\n- `DualFactoryBase<ConfigProto>`: Supports both downstream and upstream filter configurations\\n\\n- `ExceptionFreeFactoryBase<ConfigProto>`: Returns `absl::StatusOr` instead of throwing exceptions\\n\\n**Example: BufferFilter** (`source/extensions/filters/http/buffer/config.h`):\\n- `BufferFilterFactory`: Extends `DualFactoryBase`\\n- `createFilterFactoryFromProtoTyped()`: Returns a lambda that creates `BufferFilter` instances\\n  ```cpp\\n  return [filter_config](Http::FilterChainFactoryCallbacks& callbacks) -> void {\\n    callbacks.addStreamDecoderFilter(std::make_shared<BufferFilter>(filter_config));\\n  };\\n  ```\\n- Registration via `REGISTER_FACTORY(BufferFilterFactory, NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory)`\\n\\n## 6. Request Router Filter\\n\\n**Router::FilterConfig** (`source/common/router/router.h`):\\n- Implements `Http::FilterChainFactory` for upstream HTTP filters\\n- `createFilterChain()`: Uses `FilterChainUtility::createFilterChainForFactories()` to build upstream filter chains\\n- Allows filters to be chained between the router and upstream connections\\n\\n## Registration Flow Summary\\n\\n1. **Compile Time**: Filter implementations define factory classes inheriting from `NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory`\\n2. **Static Initialization**: `REGISTER_FACTORY` macro instantiates `RegisterFactory`, which calls `FactoryRegistry<NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory>::registerFactory()`\\n3. **Configuration Time**: Server parses config, `FilterChainHelper` looks up factories by name and calls `createFilterFactoryFromProto()` to create filter callbacks\\n4. **Per-Stream Time**: `FilterManager::createFilterChain()` is called, which invokes cached `FilterFactoryCb` callbacks\\n5. **Per-Stream**: Each callback creates actual filter instances and registers them with `FilterChainManager`\\n\\nThis design separates concerns: factories handle expensive operations (parsing, validation) at configuration time, while actual filter instantiation happens lazily per-stream.\"\n}","is_error":false}]},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"f51894fb-3b87-4982-bb16-537c9f5cce15","uuid":"ab4d09ad-c9fc-4737-baeb-47915f1d92d3","tool_use_result":{"stdout":"
